The ILL_INPUT flag will also be returned if the linear solver routine CV--- (called by the user after calling CVodeCreate) failed to set one of the linear solver-related fields in cvode_mem or if the linear solver's init routine failed. In any case, the user should see the printed error message for more details.; In virtual double rr::CVODEIntegrator::integrate(double, double)```</details>|
